  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_568d62ce-8cc1-41a3-8bd8-56c13bc053b7'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

    <a title="Bookgirl Book Blogger" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/83628214-bookgirl-book-blogger"><img alt="Bookgirl Book Blogger" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557208564p2/83628214.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2438934853?book_show_action=true">Jul 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bookgirl Book Blogger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bookgirl Book Blogger" href="/user/show/83628214-bookgirl-book-blogger">Bookgirl Book Blogger</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition B07D96CT4Q" href="/book/show/55856171-beyond-the-pale">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">people that love sexy rich men with a dark side</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/83628214-bookgirl-book-blogger?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2438934853" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5747671865322357417">A beautiful, sad story about true love.<br/><br/>Beyond the Pale is one of the most beautiful and heartfelt stories I've ever had the privilege of reading - to start with.....then IT happened. I flick back over chapters every now and then and fall even more in love with this story, even though the twist is like WTF didn't see that coming. <br/><br/>Amelia's childhood is quite traumatic, no child should ever have to endure that suffering. <br/>If you don't read the whole book, you won't understand the story as it all unf</span>
  <span id="freeText5747671865322357417" style="display:none">A beautiful, sad story about true love.<br /><br />Beyond the Pale is one of the most beautiful and heartfelt stories I've ever had the privilege of reading - to start with.....then IT happened. I flick back over chapters every now and then and fall even more in love with this story, even though the twist is like WTF didn't see that coming. <br /><br />Amelia's childhood is quite traumatic, no child should ever have to endure that suffering. <br />If you don't read the whole book, you won't understand the story as it all unfolds towards the end. I'll admit, I wondered what the fuss was half way through but as the story developed you realize something pretty horrific must have happened for Amelia to be the way she is. I didn't realize how far her depravity ran. There were times I cried like a baby and also times I laughed, I just loved the banter between the two characters. I even jumped up and yelled "no!"<br /><br />With all that being said, I loved this story and cannot wait to see what happens next.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5747671865322357417" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Guy willingly toys with her emotions and pushes the boundaries of pain and pleasure. <br /><br />But, when nightmares of her past torment her, she finds herself seeking answers, believing they will lead her to an unsolved case. Her determined probing and obsession has placed her in mortal danger and she realises that to lure the opposition she must use someone as bait. Herself.<br /><br /><u> Can Amelia make her crucial breakthrough before it's too late? </u></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15286985098948106594">Strong for a debut. I found it was quite well-written, and from a female first-person perspective. The only trouble with that is that you know the protagonist is going to live. However, on the other side of the coin you're tapping directly into the person's first-hand emotional experience and trust me, it gets emotional! There was a lot of description and technical detail, almost like watching a film which I could get used to and I liked how the author showed these details in conversation. I als</span>
  <span id="freeText15286985098948106594" style="display:none">Strong for a debut. I found it was quite well-written, and from a female first-person perspective. The only trouble with that is that you know the protagonist is going to live. However, on the other side of the coin you're tapping directly into the person's first-hand emotional experience and trust me, it gets emotional! There was a lot of description and technical detail, almost like watching a film which I could get used to and I liked how the author showed these details in conversation. I also liked how Amelia in the beginning is quite naive and how she grows in confidence. <br /><br />What I also enjoyed was that it was set in Washington, D.C. I gave a four star because it is the debut and like a lot of debuts there are some errors but easily fixed and not any that affected my reading in anyway.<br /><br />There was some to-ing and fro-ing but by the end of the book it all made sense.</span>

I found some parts very thrilling and gory and yet other parts ro</span>
  <span id="freeText1616412345793889046" style="display:none">Downloaded the book about two weeks ago looking for something to read while EJ Wood is writing her next book. I enjoyed it very much. It's very descriptive, though sometimes a little long winded explaining medical procedures and surroundings etc. but if you're not from a medical background then at least Wood explains what she's on about so you have some understanding, so I can understand why in some aspects it is over descriptive. I found some parts very thrilling and gory and yet other parts romantic and other parts upsetting. <br /><br />Characters and plot lines are well formed with room for story line development.<br /><br />I hope the sequel is just as good! <br /><br />The subtle and often not so subtle humour kept me turning pages, and what a dramatic ending!</span>

    <a title="Nick Hall" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/85387160-nick-hall"><img alt="Nick Hall" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551782993p2/85387160.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2526544190" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7996658222652176837">This is the first book I have read by EJ Wood and for the criminal aspect of the book, it is safe to say that Wood has done me proud. It has everything needed to make a good erotic crime thriller, so many twists and turns, characters with in depth personas that kept me on the edge of my seat. It constantly added new questions and for me the mystery was great. It came to a wonderful ending where I hope there will be a sequel.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

Wood weaved in a secondary plot flawlessly so that the reader is suddenly aware that there is another even more mysterious story line than the first. I really enjoyed the ending, what a surprise! It totally took me off guard. It took me a while to get deep into it, the start takes some concentration but overall a great unusual read.</span>

    <a title="Dixie Johnson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/92946655-dixie-johnson"><img alt="Dixie Johnson" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dixie Johnson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dixie Johnson" href="/user/show/92946655-dixie-johnson">Dixie Johnson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2740414514" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4969703481108476553">5 * Love love love<br/>I love this story. Guy Davidson may I? I think this whole story is out of this world.<br/>Spoiler alert:<br/>It’s about a medical graduate Amelia Sharpe who moves to Washington, D.C to further her career at the Smithsonian. Whilst living in a prestigious cul-de-sac she meets prominent businessman Guy Davidson who moves in next door. Amelia is naive and succumbs to Guy’s temptations and finds herself overwhelmed by this possessive and somewhat controlling handsome man. Her feelings bring </span>
  <span id="freeText4969703481108476553" style="display:none">5 * Love love love<br />I love this story. Guy Davidson may I? I think this whole story is out of this world.<br />Spoiler alert:<br />It’s about a medical graduate Amelia Sharpe who moves to Washington, D.C to further her career at the Smithsonian. Whilst living in a prestigious cul-de-sac she meets prominent businessman Guy Davidson who moves in next door. Amelia is naive and succumbs to Guy’s temptations and finds herself overwhelmed by this possessive and somewhat controlling handsome man. Her feelings bring up some terrors from a past she had hoped to have escaped from and puts her new found relationship at risk. Convinced she is about to uncover an unsolved mystery she places herself in mortal danger and when a colleague crosses the line Amelia finds out that not all that meets the eye is true. The novel is taken from the pov of Amelia Sharpe and I love how she battles with her inner demons. I also love the fact she fights against her feelings towards Guy. It really does make you wonder how far you would go to for someone you love.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4969703481108476553" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8603192912581781918">Gets a definite thumbs up I decided to give this book a read and incorporated a musical dimension, when a piece of music was mentioned I quickly youtubed it whilst I read that passage and it added a whole new dimension and tone to the story. I heard about this book through a friend and it captivated me from page one. It was a twist on the usual romantic interlude with a wealthy attractive guy. There is a lot of emotion in this book so beware!</span>

At the local library a member of staff handed me Beyond the Pale. “Not for me” I explained. <br/>Another member of staff walked over and said “that book must be good, my daughter is reading that.”<br/>I thought it would be something the wife would enjoy so I bought it.<br/>As I went to checkout, the cashier gave me a cheeky wink as she passed it through. “OK what’s it about?”</span>
  <span id="freeText4940863987373349209" style="display:none"><br /><br /><br />5* A good dirty book<br />I purchased this book out of curiosity. Whilst browsing for something to read and something to pick up for the wife. At the local library a member of staff handed me Beyond the Pale. “Not for me” I explained. <br />Another member of staff walked over and said “that book must be good, my daughter is reading that.”<br />I thought it would be something the wife would enjoy so I bought it.<br />As I went to checkout, the cashier gave me a cheeky wink as she passed it through. “OK what’s it about?” I asked. She had to of read it with that expression.<br />“If you haven’t read it, I won’t spoil it.” She answered.<br />These women were all different age groups so I raised my brow and thought “mmm”<br />I could go on. I decided to read it before the wife and I was pleasantly surprised about Amelia. However, how anyone guy would ever find one like her is only in one’s imagination. I also found it great that they came together and conquered the challenges they faced. <br />After finishing Beyond the Pale, I conclude that my strange winks were put down to my devilish good looks? And somewhat resemblance to Mr Davidson – that’s my excuse anyway. I found it a good twisty dirty book.</span>

<div id="review_2751441773" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2751441773" />
    <a title="Erin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/94832260-erin"><img alt="Erin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555231613p2/94832260.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2751441773?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erin" href="/user/show/94832260-erin">Erin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Loves comtemporary romance thrillers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/94832260-erin?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/94832260-erin?shelf=romance-thriller">romance-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/94832260-erin?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/94832260-erin?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/94832260-erin?shelf=erotic">erotic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2751441773" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer585573349708460290"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/40489755.Beyond_the_Pale__Amelia_Sharpe_1_' title='Beyond the Pale (Amelia Sharpe 1) by E.J. Wood' rel='nofollow noopener'>Beyond the Pale:</a><br/><br/>First <b>Beyond the Pale</b> reread was a success! I Loved it just as much the second time around. E.J Wood certainly knows how to create and sustain an edge-of-your seat, tension-filled romance. <br/><br/>When Guy and Amelia meet there is an intense connection. Guy is a rich successful and mysterious man. It turns out that Mr Davidson has a dark side and this intrigues the younger Ms Sharpe. The book is told from Amelia Sharpe’s point of view and I found her emotions very real. I can relate to h</span>
  <span id="freeText585573349708460290" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/40489755.Beyond_the_Pale__Amelia_Sharpe_1_" title="Beyond the Pale (Amelia Sharpe 1) by E.J. Wood" rel="nofollow noopener">Beyond the Pale:</a><br /><br />First <b>Beyond the Pale</b> reread was a success! I Loved it just as much the second time around. E.J Wood certainly knows how to create and sustain an edge-of-your seat, tension-filled romance. <br /><br />When Guy and Amelia meet there is an intense connection. Guy is a rich successful and mysterious man. It turns out that Mr Davidson has a dark side and this intrigues the younger Ms Sharpe. The book is told from Amelia Sharpe’s point of view and I found her emotions very real. I can relate to her insecurities and naivety in a new relationship.<br /><br />As both of their emotions develop and they begin to fall in love, Amelia’s past returns to haunt her and does not allow her to recognize her feelings and just believes Guy is not who he says he is. <br /><br />This novel is very psychological and you really do wonder what to believe as does our Amelia. Her love for Guy is deep rooted and sometimes we need to listen to our hearts and not our heads. But can she tolerate the demands and secrecy of Mr Davidson?<br /><br />Amelia’s past is drip fed and sparse and we know very little of the eluded Mr Davidson and I really want to know more about him. He intrigues me as I imagine he did Amelia. I found their banter and jokes very funny.<br /><br />Amelia and Guy are very opposite, Amelia is an emotional woman and has a fiery temper but very rarely surfaces; she's learnt how to hide her emotions because she believes it makes her weak. Guy suppresses his temper, but we soon find out what sets it off. <br /><br />I’m so glad there is a sequel following and I admit I did shed a tear now and then. Thank you EJ Wood, this certainly is added to one of my “mind boggling seductive books” lists.<br /><br />Please hurry up on the second part.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="585573349708460290" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2791649551" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4427358484214159368"><b> Beyond the Pale is packed with passion.</b><br/><br/>This sad love story is full of charm, soul mates, combined with eroticism. It will captivate you, obsess you and possess you. <br/>I was a bit hesitant giving this book a read. But I'm so glad I did. Mr Davidson is the perfect man that keeps you on your feet, full of mystery and allure. Amelia is naive and innocent but finds strength. I hated Mr Cross, but who wouldn't? I loved the suspense, the edge of the seat page turning story. Guy's involvement at the zoo </span>
  <span id="freeText4427358484214159368" style="display:none"><b> Beyond the Pale is packed with passion.</b><br /><br />This sad love story is full of charm, soul mates, combined with eroticism. It will captivate you, obsess you and possess you. <br />I was a bit hesitant giving this book a read. But I'm so glad I did. Mr Davidson is the perfect man that keeps you on your feet, full of mystery and allure. Amelia is naive and innocent but finds strength. I hated Mr Cross, but who wouldn't? I loved the suspense, the edge of the seat page turning story. Guy's involvement at the zoo makes for a wonderful backstory that´s cleverly incorporated and the diversity of the characters gave dimension. <br />I´d recommend this to anyone that loves a hot steamy romance without the predictability of the ending.</span>

<div id="review_2804197222" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2804197222" />
    <a title="Troris" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/96677775-troris"><img alt="Troris" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1556636361p2/96677775.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2804197222?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Troris" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Troris" href="/user/show/96677775-troris">Troris</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2804197222" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10782339743454990048">I really enjoyed this book. Two worlds melt together when Amelia Sharpe meets businessman Mr Davidson and shortly after embark on a passionate love affair.<br/><br/>Between the lines there's a past that resurfaces. A past that Amelia wanted to leave behind.<br/><br/>What are we getting ourselves into when we meet someone? Can you trust your instincts? Will your heart rule your head? <br/><br/>I love Amelia, she scared me at times but I definitely want to read more.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_2615205092" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2615205092" />
    <a title="Dani" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/90172308-dani"><img alt="Dani" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1543946445p2/90172308.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2615205092?book_show_action=true">Dec 04, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dani" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dani" href="/user/show/90172308-dani">Dani</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2615205092" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2105483320707549597">Unique, dark and quirky<br/><br/>*SPOILERS*<br/><br/>Amelia clearly has had a traumatic childhood, which might go to explain why she is the way she is and when she meets the handsome man next door it brings back some memories she had hoped to have forgotten. I think deep down Amelia is a sexual deviant and enjoys the attention from Guy she so lacked from her childhood but hates being out of control and this she battles with.<br/><br/>The book is written from the perspective of that from Amelia and starts with a prologue that</span>
  <span id="freeText2105483320707549597" style="display:none">Unique, dark and quirky<br /><br />*SPOILERS*<br /><br />Amelia clearly has had a traumatic childhood, which might go to explain why she is the way she is and when she meets the handsome man next door it brings back some memories she had hoped to have forgotten. I think deep down Amelia is a sexual deviant and enjoys the attention from Guy she so lacked from her childhood but hates being out of control and this she battles with.<br /><br />The book is written from the perspective of that from Amelia and starts with a prologue that as you read on realize is a traumatic scene later on in the book, or was it? <br /><br />Amelia loves her job as a Forensic Pathologist and as an attractive young woman she is subjected to harassment; I really feel for her at this particular moment in the novel and gritted my teeth and love the empowerment she discovered, I think I would of stabbed that bastard too!<br /><br />Beyond the Pale certainly dares to be different, I was really shocked to the ending. I never would of guessed the outcome and neither the inner strength Amelia found. I also found it quite interesting how everything I had read I really believed and yet towards the end it just shows that not everything is as it is if you have just seen it develop from one perspective. I found that twist quite cleverly written.<br /><br />Amelia's confidence improves in the novel and I think the Author's did as well. Seeing as this is a debut the author and Amelia are probably not unlike one another in the fact they try and see what they are capable of.<br /><br />Some scenes were quite vulgar and violent, the book does evolve around a love story so yes there will be sex but I didn't feel it had too much. <br /><br />I found myself smiling, laughing, cringing, nail biting and horrified and the humor kept me reading.<br /><br />I give this a 4 * STAR. I knocked 1 * STAR off because it isn't perfect. There are some errors, although for an indie book I don't mind that so much. Even some top publishers' books have errors. However my rating is because it is a little to and fro (reality / nightmares / past) and my english literacy is a little rusty so the poetic references to Shakespeare I tended to skip by on.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2105483320707549597" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('i29x0GDsOGw1rb4lutWJcPRkYISSjRrnY+WXiDfeg70iV4VKr+l0h4kKUbgd5CJGlwgTwLEHRO0rvqgS8DXQdA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_231604').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_231604').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_231604').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>
